### Frage: Wie viele Semester dauert das Bachelor Studium?

**Status**: `200` | **Dauer**: `5.81s`

**Antwort:**
```
Das Bachelorstudium dauert sieben Semester.

{"id": "4", "entity": "Wirtschaftsinformatik", "type": "category", "description": "Wirtschaftsinformatik is a specialized academic field of study that combines the principles of computer science with those of business administration. It is frequently offered as a focused degree program, often as a Bachelor‚Äôs degree, within the Faculty of Business Information Systems and is commonly studied at institutions such as the University of Bayreuth and Universit√§t Heidelberg, particularly during the Internationale Woche. The core of Wirtschaftsinformatik examines the application of computer science to economic problems, focusing on the economic use of data and information systems. This encompasses business information processing and delivery, data analysis, database management, and business process optimization. [{"id": "1", "entity": "Informatik", "type": "category", "description": "Informatik is a broad field of study encompassing computer science and the art of computing. It represents a significant degree program and a recognized career path, established 40 years ago by Wolfgang Fischer and presently supported by the Professor Wolfgang Maria Fischer Stiftung. The discipline investigates the workings of digital computers and the broader discipline of information processing, covering areas such as programming, data structures, algorithms, binary arithmetic, Boolean algebra, formal languages, automata models (including Moore and Mealy automata), and the functionalities of the Internet and World Wide Web. Specifically, Informatik addresses critical aspects of modern computing, including software and systems development, effective management of information and communication systems, data analysis and decision-making support, and increasingly, cybersecurity and data protection. The study program is offered at several universities, including the Department of Computer Science and Business Information Systems at the University of W√ºrzburg, the Fachhochschule St. P√∂lten, Universit√§t Heidelberg, and the University of Bayreuth during the Internationale Woche. Students in Informatik study data persistence, utilizing both Relational Database Management Systems (RDBMS) and exploring techniques without them, and the discipline is the subject area of the ### Frage: Welche Buslinien fahren zum Standort SHL?

**Status**: `200` | **Dauer**: `5.85s`

**Antwort:**
```
Welche Buslinien fahren zum Standort SHL? Die Buslinie 214 startet am Busbahnhof (Bussteig 2, vor dem Hauptbahnhof W√ºrzburg) und braucht bis zur Endhaltestelle SHL ca. 20 Minuten. Abends oder am Wochenende nutzen Sie bitte die Buslinien 110 oder 114, die bis zur Haltestelle vor der Julius-Maximilians-Universit√§t W√ºrzburg am Hubland fahren. Von dort ben√∂tigen Sie ca. 10 Minuten zu Fu√ü zum Standort SHL. Nutzen Sie die Fahrplanauskunft des Verkehrsunternehmens-Verbund Mainfranken GmbH.
```
